The Inland Debt Bondholders Association Telegraphed for Resistance to Northeast Customs 152

Sovereignty Cannot Be Infringed by Others

The Inland Public Debt Bondholders Association telegraphed to Nanjing yesterday, saying: To the Executive Yuan, Ministry of Finance, and Ministry of Foreign Affairs of the National Government of Nanjing: It is reported that the Northeast puppet state, at the instigation of the Japanese, forcibly seizes customs duties, and the people are indignant. Customs duties guarantee the funds for domestic and foreign debts, which are the basis of international credit to the outside world and the lifeline of domestic finance, which is of great importance. Northeast tax revenue amounts to 40 million yuan per year. If the debt credit is shaken due to the seizure, what a terrible disaster it would cause! Moreover, customs administration is a part of sovereignty, how can it be infringed by others? We earnestly request serious resistance to protect sovereignty and maintain national credit. We are filled with eager anticipation. The Inland Public Debt Bondholders Association respectfully salutes. Seal.

This City is Preparing for Autonomy 153

The Municipal Government Announces the Rules of the Preparatory Committee

The Shanghai Municipal Government yesterday announced the rules of the Shanghai Municipal Autonomy Preparatory Committee as follows: Article 1. This committee concurrently assumes the responsibility of the Shanghai Municipal Government to handle preparatory matters for autonomy at all levels below the district in this city. Article 2. This committee shall have seven members, appointed by the mayor from among the officials of the various organs under the municipal government, and one person shall be designated as chairman. Article 3. This committee may establish branch offices. Each branch office shall have one director and one to two deputy directors, who shall be subject to the direction and supervision of this committee and assist in all matters. The rules for the branch offices shall be determined separately. Article 4. This committee shall establish the following three groups, each with one director, several staff members, and secretaries: (A) General Affairs Group, whose duties are as follows: (1) drafting, copying, proofreading, receiving, and dispatching documents; (2) keeping and using the seal; (3) personnel attendance, assessment, rewards, and punishments; (4) general affairs and accounting matters; (5) recording meeting minutes; (6) business statistics; (7) compiling and publicizing matters; (8) other matters not belonging to other groups; (B) Investigation Group, whose duties are as follows: (1) investigation and demarcation of boundaries; (2) investigation, review, and sampling of household registrations; (3) surveying and mapping boundary maps and explanations; (4) statistics and compilation of household registration surveys; (5) other related investigation matters; (C) Election Group, whose duties are as follows: (1) planning and preparing for district, neighborhood, and lane elections; (2) supervising and guiding district, neighborhood, and lane elections; (3) publicizing matters related to elections; (4) reviewing and compiling voter lists; (5) other matters related to elections. Article 5. Members of this committee may concurrently serve as directors of various groups. Article 6. In addition to personnel transferred from the municipal government and its subordinate organs, this committee's staff may be employed with the approval of the municipal government. Article 7. This committee shall hold regular meetings once a week, and temporary meetings may be convened by the chairman when necessary. Article 8. This committee must have the attendance of more than two-thirds of the members to hold a formal meeting. Article 9. If the chairman is unable to attend the meeting of this committee due to any reason, he shall entrust another member to act as his agent. Article 10. The regular and business expenses required by this committee shall be compiled into a general budget and submitted to the municipal government for monthly allocation. Article 11. The preparation period for this committee is tentatively set at three months, and the autonomous organizations at all levels below the district shall be completed within the time limit. If there are special circumstances, and it is possible to complete the work on schedule, a request shall be submitted to the municipal government for an appropriate extension. Article 12. The detailed rules for this committee's operations shall be determined separately. Article 13. If there are any matters not covered in these rules, they may be submitted to the municipal government for revision at any time. Article 14. These rules shall be implemented from the date of announcement by the Shanghai Municipal Government.

The Sugar Industry Association Reported that Japanese Sugar is Being Shipped to Hankou in Large Quantities 154

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Sent a Letter to the Hankou Chamber of Commerce for Secret Investigation

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, based on a report from the Sugar Industry Association that Japanese sugar is being shipped to Hankou in large quantities, sent a letter to the Hankou Municipal Chamber of Commerce requesting a ban on buying and selling. The letter stated: Dear Sirs, on the 22nd of this month, this city's Sugar Industry Association sent a letter stating: "We believe that violent Japan has not repented of its disasters, and for the sake of survival, our nation's economic severance from Japan should not be abandoned halfway. Moreover, the black soil of the Northeast is still occupied by foreign lands, and the Shanghai soil is still stained with blood. It is the time for us to endure hardship and learn from the pain. We have received reliable information that Japanese trading houses in this port have recently shipped large quantities of Japanese sugar to Hankou. After this sugar arrives in Hankou, it must be sold by a small number of traitors among Chinese merchants, who disregard shame and serve the enemy. If we do not take measures to prevent it, what a terrible disaster it will cause. Our association is deeply concerned and dare not remain silent. Therefore, we earnestly request your association to examine and approve this matter, and quickly forward it to the Hankou Municipal Chamber of Commerce, instructing the relevant trade associations to strictly prevent favoritism and effectively stop it, in order to implement the main objective of economic severance from Japan." Based on this, we believe that violent Japan despises our country. Although the Shanghai case has come to an end, the situation in the Northeast is becoming more and more pressing. If the people of the country have a conscience, they should encourage each other and persevere to the end on the matter of boycotting goods, so that we may achieve the final effect. Now it is said that Japanese merchants are shipping large quantities of sugar to Hankou. If our colleagues in Hankou take this opportunity to sell it, it would not only be disregarding shame and serving the enemy, but also a cause for ridicule by the Japanese. Therefore, we are informing you of the situation and hope that your association will investigate secretly if there is a large shipment of Japanese sugar to Hankou, and inform the sugar industry to collectively prevent the purchase and sale of the sugar. This is our sincere hope.

This City's Plague Situation is Rampant This Year 155

Wu Liande Suggested Reducing Tap Water Prices

The Taxpayers Association Advocated Launching an Epidemic Prevention Campaign

Dr. Wu Liande of the Seaport Quarantine Office sent a letter to the Chinese Taxpayers Association a few days ago, with important suggestions for summer epidemic prevention. After receiving the letter, the association forwarded it to the Public Works Bureau, requesting them to take it seriously. At the same time, they also replied to Dr. Wu, advocating that the municipal government, together with the authorities of the two concessions and civil groups, launch a widespread epidemic prevention campaign for a period of one month. Excerpts from the two letters are recorded below:

Reply to Wu Liande's Letter: Dear Sir, we have received your letter, expressing concern for the health of the people and valuing human life, which we greatly admire. Your various proposals are all essential measures, and our association has forwarded them to the Public Works Bureau, requesting them to pay serious attention to them. However, our association has even further thoughts, believing that at this time, after the war and with the hot summer approaching, the spread of cholera is extremely worrying. The Shanghai Municipal Government should unite the Public Concession, the French Concession authorities, and civil groups to launch a widespread epidemic prevention campaign for a period of one month, so that the general public can understand the importance of prevention, and perhaps achieve a greater effect. Whether this is feasible, we would appreciate your consideration. Sincerely,

Letter to the Public Works Bureau: Dear Sir, we have received a letter from Wu Liande, Director of the Seaport Quarantine Management Office and Director of the Central Cholera Prevention Office, stating that the cholera situation in Shanghai this year is not only earlier than in previous years, but also more rampant than in the past. From April 26, the date of the first case, until last week (June 11), a total of 280 cases of cholera were seen, but in the past week alone, there have been as many as 240 cases reported. The duty of this office is to do everything possible to prevent and avoid the spread of the epidemic, together with the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau, the Public Concession, and the French Concession Health Department. However, the spread of the epidemic cannot be successful without the joint cooperation of all sectors and the entire public. Fortunately, it is not yet the hottest summer, and it is urgent to take precautions early to avoid the spread. The weekly cholera reports published by this office are nothing more than to awaken the public's attention to prevention. But in my opinion, the origin of cholera in Shanghai this year is (1) that laborers and the public do not have access to high-quality beverages, such as poor people not being able to afford expensive tap water; (2) the entire public should be advised to get vaccinated and cooperate with health authorities to disinfect latrines; (3) wells and rivers in remote areas should also be disinfected, and the public should be advised not to drink raw water or eat cut-up fresh fruit sold in the market. Other measures, such as finding ways to dispose of garbage and eliminate flies, are also necessary to address this cholera outbreak. The above-mentioned matters have been repeatedly elaborated in this office's weekly reports. Western newspapers have all rushed to publish them, but many Chinese newspapers still ignore them. Considering that your bureau is concerned about the interests of the people and social public undertakings, we hereby inform you and request that you quickly unite all sectors, discuss with the Chinese and Foreign Concession Water Companies to dredge the water pipes and reduce water prices, so that the poor people can enjoy clean beverages together. Secondly, advise the public to pay close attention to vaccination and latrine disinfection and natural water disinfection. The health authorities will naturally be responsible for guidance, but the public's facilities are very simple. I, Liande, have always been concerned about the public health movement, so I must thoroughly study the root causes of every event that occurs and find the best solutions. Whether my suggestions are appropriate, I hope you will consider them carefully. Upon this, we believe that Dr. Wu Liande's proposed methods for preventing cholera are indeed essential measures. At this time, with the hot summer approaching and after the war, if we do not take active measures, we fear that the spread will be difficult to control. We should request that the Water Company adopt the suggestions of dredging the water pipes and reducing the water prices, and at the same time instruct the Health Department to step up work on vaccination and various disinfections, broadcast announcements, prohibit the sale of cut-up fresh fruits and unhygienic cold drinks, and properly dispose of garbage to emphasize hygiene. This is our sincere hope.

Yangtze River's Great Wall-Like Embankment Completed 161

The Greatest Project After the Great Wall

Constructed by 660,000 Disaster Relief Workers

The Yangtze River Will Be Free From Floods Forever

Last year's floods caused disasters in sixteen provinces, and more than 47 million people were displaced. After August 2nd, Wuhan was submerged in floods, and hundreds of thousands of refugees were taken in by Beijing and Shanghai. The government established a Flood Relief Committee and allocated funds for relief. At the same time, it used work as a form of relief, building a Great Wall-like embankment to fundamentally address the problem of flooding. This year, the river water continues to rise, and recent storms and heavy rains have raised the Yangtze River water level again. People are worried about being submerged again, but according to reporters' investigations, the Flood Relief Committee's Great Wall-like embankment is about to be completed. From now on, the Yangtze River will be free from floods forever. The fact that the people in the disaster areas of Anhui, Jiangxi, and Hubei provinces have not been completely dyed red this year is entirely due to the completion of this embankment, which allows the disaster areas to continue to cultivate and farm. The reporter's findings are detailed below:

Motivation for Building the Embankment: The Work Relief Office attached to the Flood Relief Committee planned water management projects and hired Xi Dejiong as the chief engineer. After investigating the floods in various ports along the Yangtze River, it was found that the breaches and collapses of the original embankments caused last year's unprecedented disaster. The fundamental solution for future flood prevention is to rebuild new and strong embankments along the Yangtze River. After the decision was made, 260 to 270 engineering experts were sent to the upper and lower reaches of the Yangtze River to design the embankment construction.

Establishment of Bureaus for Management: After the designs were finalized, the Work Relief Office began work. The Yangtze River embankment was divided into sections starting from Shashi in the upper reaches, passing through Hankou, Jiujiang, Anqing, Datong, Wuhu, and all the way to Twelve Shoals in Yangzhou, winding for more than 10,000 miles, all being constructed simultaneously. Along the Yangtze River, 18 supervisory bureaus for embankment construction and work relief were established. Construction began last winter, and all engineering matters were under the jurisdiction of the Work Relief Office of the Shanghai Water Conservancy Committee.

Recruitment of Disaster Relief Workers: The long embankment along the river was rushed to be built in the spring of this year. 660,000 disaster victims from Jiangsu, Anhui, Jiangxi, and Hubei provinces were selected by the Flood Relief Committee and assigned to different sections to start construction. More than 1,100 supervisory committee members were also employed to supervise the progress. A large portion of the 430,000 tons of disaster relief wheat and flour purchased by the central government from the United States was allocated for the construction of the embankment. The relief method was calculated based on an area of 100 cubic feet of embankment. For every square of embankment built, the Work Relief Office provided 7.5 catties of relief wheat. The total amount of relief wheat distributed for the entire embankment required tens of thousands of tons.

Completion of the Embankment: The length of the embankment reaches more than 10,000 miles, and the area and height of the embankment are more than 20 English feet. The embankment construction is also very solid. Because there are many disaster relief workers and the construction is divided into sections, it has been completely completed to this day. The Flood Relief Committee will therefore be closed at the end of this month. According to the committee's announcement, although the tide has risen this year, the water level in Hankou is currently three feet and two inches and seven points, which is still far from last year. Even if it rises again, it can be guaranteed that the Yangtze River will never see floods again.

Dredging the Huai River: Last year, the Huai River breached, and northern Jiangsu also suffered floods. Dredging the Huai River has been loudly advocated for a long time, but no funds have been available to carry it out, resulting in the fertile land on both sides of the Huai River being abandoned. Now, while the Flood Relief Committee is building embankments along the Yangtze River, the Work Relief Office has also assigned more than 80,000 disaster victims from northern Jiangsu to dredge the Huai River, and a batch of relief wheat has been allocated from the disaster relief wheat for the Work Relief Branch to be responsible for carrying out the project. A total of three branches have been established, and more than 40 hydraulic engineering experts and more than 200 supervisory personnel have been hired. They are currently supervising the dredging work. From now on, hundreds of thousands of acres of wasteland on both sides of the Huai River will be turned into fertile land in one fell swoop, which will bring great production benefits to the country and the people.

Zhu Qinglan Telegraphed the Grand Ceremony for the Completion of the Jinghui Canal 162

Zhu Ziqiao, Director of the Disaster Area Work Group of the National Government's Flood Relief Committee, telegraphed: Brothers Zhang Peilao, Cha Mianzhong, Xi Mingjiu, and Jin Guanfu of the Disaster Area Work Group, arrived in Xi'an on the afternoon of the 19th. On the 20th, they participated in the completion and water release ceremony of the Jinghui Canal at Junerzui in northern Wei. After inspecting along the canal, the water flowed smoothly, and the people were drawing water from the canal for irrigation with joy. The local people, young and old, who visited the canal construction were even more delighted and encouraged, and the road was blocked. Moreover, due to the recent severe drought in Guanzhong, the people were terrified of the disasters of previous years, and the demand for rain was extremely urgent. Although the people of the five counties have benefited from the Jing Canal, the people in other counties such as Wu, Fu, Qian, and Li, who are suffering from drought, are even more eager for rain. Witnessing the disaster, I am even more anxious. Declaration of the Support Association for the Northeast War 168

So Painful It Cannot Be Read to the End

The Shanghai All-Circles Support Association for Northeast Soldiers issued a serious declaration on saving the country: All compatriots across the country, please be aware: Since the Japanese imperialists invaded our country, the Bixue case in Wanbaoshan has not yet dried, and the entire three northeastern provinces have been lost to non-resistant soldiers. Although the flames of war in Shanghai have temporarily stopped, the 30 million compatriots in the Northeast are still suffering in the depths of water and fire under the oppression of the brutal Japanese invaders. Death and burning are beyond the imagination of compatriots in the mainland. Alas, the country is dying day by day, how can we live? All my hot-blooded compatriots should endure hardship, save food and clothing, carry guns and transport money, and rise up to save the country. In the face of great disaster, empty talk is useless. Sacrificing oneself in danger is the way to become an adult. (Omission) Compatriots, the country has reached this point. What can't we give up to our compatriots? What benefit can't we throw away? And there are things that cannot be said. Whenever a large number of patriotic compatriots gather to talk, they all say that we, the civilians who have no weapons, how can we resist the strong enemy's artillery fire? Although the saying is close to reason, it can only be understood in a tangible way. National men and women compatriots of the unarmed class, if everyone does not buy or sell enemy goods, they can control the enemy's military expenses and the ability to manufacture guns and artillery. Especially the national business community, as the armed comrades of the business war in recent centuries, their intangible resistance to the enemy is even better than tangible guns and artillery. It's not that they can't do it, it's that they don't do it. Wearing enemy clothing is like wearing the bloody clothes of the armed compatriots on the front line. Eating enemy food is like eating the flesh and blood of the martyred compatriots. In short, the compatriots in the Northeast who are suffering and the armed compatriots who are fighting the enemy day and night in the rain of guns and bullets, why are they not our family members? After all, they are all descendants of the Yellow Emperor. Don't say that the three northeastern provinces are far away from our hometown, how can we not know that the brutal enemy's planes and warships can be overhead at any time? If the boots are burned, the body will be burned. If the country is lost, the family will be destroyed, and we will all be slaves. If the skin does not exist, what will the hair be attached to? We hope that compatriots across the country will contribute money to help the army, or raise money to purchase national defense weapons. Those who have no money should stand up and kill the enemy, and send people to promote it everywhere. The life and death of the country, the honor and disgrace of our descendants, are in a critical moment. If we let it go, it will be too late. The members of this association are willing to be pioneers and hereby declare.

Recent Miserable Situation of the Disaster in Shaanxi Province 174

The Chinese Jishng Hui received letters yesterday from the counties of Chang'an, Wugong, Fufeng, Jingyang, Liquan, and Qianxian in Shaanxi Province, and according to the report from the Chang'an Branch of the Association, the three years of non-stop disasters have left people unable to catch their breath, and drought has come again. In March of this year, during the growth period of spring wheat, the weather suddenly turned cold, black frost fell repeatedly, strong winds roared, and hail fell together. Within ten days, it spread throughout the province. Afterwards, although there was a penetrating rain, the seedlings had withered and the disaster had become inevitable. There was no way to save it. According to disaster reports and appeals from all sides, it has reached more than 20 counties, and those who have broken up their families and fled famine are even more displaced and suffering, which is unbearable to see and hear. I didn't expect the past catastrophe to be repeated again. Thinking about the future, how can we imagine it? Recently, we received the Shaanxi Relief Association's summary of the recent disaster situation in various counties and disaster maps. The branch association also received letters and telegrams from various counties asking for relief and immediately reported them. We beg you to widely need Hong Ci, deliver the publicity, or send letters to various places to appeal on your behalf, so as to clarify the true picture of the disaster in Shaanxi, in order to plan for relief. Central Government's Opium Prohibition Order Anti-Drug Association Issues Declaration 175

One Side Doubts, One Side Urges

The Chinese National Anti-Drug Association issued a special declaration yesterday regarding the opium prohibition order reissued by the National Government on June 18: On June 20, it was reported that the National Government ordered on the 18th, "Opium is a thing that harms the country and the people. The government is determined to ban it and has repeatedly issued orders and prohibitions. It has also successively promulgated various anti-smoking laws and regulations and set up special supervision and guidance agencies to urge progress. However, the country is vast and the examination may not be thorough. I am sincerely afraid that remote provinces will be complacent over time and fail to implement the prohibitions effectively, or blame the special circumstances of the local area and fail to eliminate the opium completely, resulting in the failure of previous efforts. Therefore, the prohibition is reissued with earnest warnings. In the future, local officials must strictly implement the current laws and regulations for the implementation of the smoking ban, and must not disobey and treat it as a mere formality. If there is still negligence, disregard for the prohibition, and harm to the local area, once discovered, the law will be enforced and punished separately." People across the country were overjoyed, thinking that the government was really reversing the chaos, working hard to govern, and saving this dangerous situation. Even this association was overjoyed when it suddenly read this order, thinking that the government has such a resolute and decisive spirit and implements policies that eliminate disadvantages. The government has a sincere intention to ban smoking. How dare we speak in vain? However, recalling the terrible facts of the past and the tragic scenes vividly in our minds, we cannot help but worry too much and dare not believe it, based on the authorities' previous inconsistent words and deeds. People are afraid of tigers, and everyone has this feeling. Punishing the past and not forgetting the past pain is the feeling that the Chinese people should have. It is not only the association. I still remember that last spring, when the theory of public opium sales was first circulating, the people across the country secretly rose up in opposition. The authorities, fearing public anger, once said, "Public opium sales are not true," to appease the people's opposition. However, within two months, "Anti-Smoking Inspection Offices" were established in various provinces. The people continued to protest, and the government announced the cancellation and reiterated the prohibition. Unexpectedly, the brewing of a disguised opium sales management agency for narcotic drugs followed one after another. How the government treats the people in this way, how can the people trust the government? Recently, the authorities have both sown the tide of public opium sales and issued an order to reiterate the ban on smoking. It is unpredictable and changes are unpredictable. Is the authorities still following their old tricks? The people are really half-believing. Moreover, as the prohibition states, "The government is determined to reject it and has repeatedly issued orders and prohibitions." The so-called "three orders and five applications" are nothing more than empty documents, based on past facts. Facts are there, how can you not be familiar with them? The so-called "the country is vast and the examination may not be thorough" The government cannot justify itself on this point. The area is remote, so let's put it aside based on the government's statement that the examination is not thorough. How far is Nanjing from the capital and the counties north of the Yangtze River? The government in the Weiyang area is everywhere. Why did the government really see it? Luoyang is located in the temporary capital, and the tobacco disaster in Henan Province is the most serious in the country. Are other provinces such as Fujian, Anhui, Hunan, and Hubei also remote places? Public opium sales were first implemented and the harm of poison spread. It is unbearable to hear. It is true that the government has never examined or has examined but deliberately kept silent. The so-called "Once discovered, the law will be enforced and punished separately" is even more irritating. It is hoped that the government can "enforce the law and punish separately." However, the government treats them with grace or allows them to be free from the law. Although the people have repeatedly appealed for legal action, the government is still silent. The association is eager to reject drugs and does not feel that the words are long. Loving the party and the country is even more important than others. We do not dare to criticize the government's decrees slightly, but we think that governing does not lie in many words, and facts are the most powerful defense. If the government has the sincere intention to ban smoking, it should take practical actions in addition to the shining orders. Moreover, rumors are very strong outside. There are anti-smoking authorities who have not given up on public opium sales and plan to adopt a policy of banning it in the open but secretly implementing it. On the one hand, they indicate that various provinces are selling it publicly and the central government will not interfere. Use its "divide and conquer" trick. Based on our observations of all parties in recent days, we cannot regard this news as absolutely unfounded. We hope that the government can eliminate the confusion of villains and strive to implement the prohibition, so as to punish the facts and show the people of the country to strengthen the people's trust in the government. The association will follow the people of the country and strongly support the government's measures to vigorously ban smoking, so as to complete the legacy of rejecting drugs. Otherwise, the members of the association will still not be able to give up their responsibilities as long as they have a breath left. I hereby declare.

Chen Longsheng Murders Ye Daxing's Wife 178

Commits Murder Out of Embarrassment for Demanding Debt

Falsely Accuses the Deceased of Immoral Behavior

Chen Longsheng, also known as Sun Rongsheng, 35 years old, from Nanjing, worked repairing burlap bags and resided at number 88, Xinkang Li, Taopeng Road. The sub-landlord was Ye Daxing. His wife, Wu, age 42. At about 8 PM on the 19th of this month, the Ye couple and fellow villagers Song Afu, Chen Caipin, and others were playing mahjong for entertainment. Wu demanded 39 yuan from Chen to use as gambling money. Chen first returned two yuan. Wu considered the amount too small and argued with him. Unexpectedly, Chen became furious and took out a small knife from his sleeve, stabbing Wu's neck and other places. Ye Daxing, seeing Chen fighting with his wife, stepped forward to dissuade him and was also stabbed in the back of the neck. When he tried to snatch the knife, the web between his thumb and forefinger was cut. He immediately ran out and called for the police. Chen took the opportunity to escape. Seeing Wu lying in a pool of blood, barely alive, she was rushed to Tongren Hospital. Due to the severity of her injuries, with nine stab wounds to her neck, she soon died. The body was taken to the Forensic Examination Office on Fairlane Road. The next morning, a prosecutor commissioned by the Special Court examined the body and ordered it to be coffined. Ye Daxing's injuries were relatively minor, and after treatment by a doctor, his life was out of danger. The day before yesterday, Hua Tan Gui Shou of the Yulin Road Police Station arrested the murderer Chen Longsheng in the Small World Amusement Park in the city and detained him at the relevant Public Security Bureau. Yesterday morning, he was brought back to the police station and escorted to the First Special District Local Court. Presiding Judge Qiao Wanxuan opened the court for interrogation. Zhang Tianyin, a lawyer from the police station, stated the case, saying that the defendant's murder weapon was hidden by him after the incident at number 333, Wuzhou Road. The defendant initially refused to confess, but after strict interrogation, he said it was under the incense burner in the house. The detectives searched but found nothing. Later, it was retrieved from a hidden ditch in the patio. He then presented the knife for inspection and requested severe punishment. Subsequently, the plaintiff Ye Daxing complained that he was the chief clerk at the Yihua Yarn Factory in Yangshupu, but his injuries were not serious. The defendant was a tenant and recounted the facts of the incident. Song Afu testified that he was a neighbor and saw the plaintiff couple and Chen Caipin playing mahjong at the time. He saw the defendant come down from upstairs to the living room to return two yuan to Ye Wu (the deceased). Because she thought it was too little, she wanted him to increase it, which led to an argument. He also wanted him to compensate for the damaged components. The defendant asked what he wanted to compensate for. Wu said you know yourself. The defendant was furious and punched Wu in the face. He suddenly saw blood flowing from Wu's neck and realized she had been injured with a weapon. Ye Daxing rushed to dissuade him and was also stabbed. Chen Caipin testified that Ye Daxing was his master. He saw the defendant return two yuan to his master's wife. Because it was too little, he wanted him to increase it but failed, which led to an argument. The defendant said that he wanted her life today, and then punched her wildly. He then took out a small knife and stabbed his master's wife, who immediately fell to the ground. When questioned, the defendant Chen Longsheng confessed that his real name was Sun Rongsheng. Because he stayed with the Chen family, he changed his name to Chen Longsheng. He had known the deceased for five years. He used to live on Meizhou Road and later moved to Xinkang Li, living together for about a year. However, Wu and Ye Daxing also had an affair. The thirty yuan he borrowed from Wu was actually usurious money. She forced him to pay it back at the time, and in a fit of anger, he stabbed her. The reason was that Wu had recently had an affair with his apprentice Chen Caipin and abandoned him. Hearing this, Ye Daxing stated that the defendant's confession was completely false. Chen Caipin said that he was only 23 years old and his master's wife was 42 years old. How could such an immoral thing happen? He asked for a clear judgment. Judge Qiao reviewed the confession and ordered the defendant to be taken back into custody for further questioning at a later date.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Asks Central Government to Eliminate Labor-Management Disputes 179

Both Sides Should Maintain Understanding and Concession

To Get Through This Unprecedented Difficult Situation

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday requested the Party and government organs to eliminate labor-management disputes and increase production, and submitted a petition to the Central Party Headquarters, stating that the association held the third session of its members' meeting on June 18. According to the proposals of members Luo Qinghua, Tu Kaizheng, Pan Xusheng, Lu Fengzhu, Zheng Chengqing, Ye Jiaxing, Wang Yansong, Xie Zhongle, Ma Shaoquan, Shao Baoxing, Shen Jisi, Wang Zefu, etc., it was requested that the Central Government issue an order to all local Party and government organs to earnestly eliminate labor-management disputes, increase the production of domestic goods, and cultivate strength to save the country from its difficulties. It was resolved and submitted to the Central Government for approval. It has been found that in recent years, the provinces of Yu, Anhui, Jiangxi, and Hubei have been severely disrupted by Communist bandits, and the rural organizations have long been completely destroyed. The northwestern provinces have also been plagued by years of severe drought, and villages have become ruins. The provinces of Hebei and Shandong are relatively complete, but since the three provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang were occupied by Japan, the road for the two provinces to immigrate to Guanwai has also been cut off. As for the two provinces of Jiangsu and Zhejiang, they are still slightly better in the southeast, but due to the poor harvest of silkworms, the closure of silk factories, and the war in the Songhu-Jiatai area, workers have lost their jobs, and farmers have abandoned silkworm rearing, which has also become a precarious situation. This phenomenon, recursively promoted and developed, will inevitably turn all the good people of the country into starving corpses and bandits. This is truly the most serious situation in the past 20 years of the Republic of China. Although European and American countries have been thrown into unprecedented panic by unemployment problems, the foundation of their industrial countries has been consolidated, and overseas markets are sufficient to rely on as a retreat. The recovery of vitality is still easy to deal with. If our country has no industrial base and the countryside is on the verge of collapse, the degree of difference is no different from the sky. At this time, if we want to seek a way to remedy the situation, we can only strive to produce, so that workers have jobs and agricultural products have sales channels. Then, the national livelihood may be transformed from thorns into a smooth road. In this stormy situation, labor and management should maintain mutual understanding and concession in order to overcome this unprecedented difficult situation. The Party and government organs that handle labor-management disputes should also take into account the current situation in our country and not pursue lofty theories anymore, so that those with some financial resources will not be afraid of engaging in industry and that the habit of concentrating cash in one corner of the city and concentrating investment in the concession real estate can be gradually changed. Otherwise, it will be like Jia Yi said, "If you don't cure it now, it will become a chronic disease. If you can't secure the interior, how can you talk about resisting foreign aggression?" All of the above, the cultivation of national power, is intended to start with earnestly eliminating labor-management disputes and increasing the production of domestic goods. It is reasonable to prepare a document and submit it to the Cabinet for review and approval for implementation, which is truly convenient for the public. Respectfully presented to the Central Party Headquarters.

The Shanghai Municipal Porcelain Industry Association submitted a document to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, stating that it recently received a letter dated June 7 from the Preparatory Office of the Jingdezhen Jing City Porcelain Merchants Association of Jiangxi, stating that the Jiangxi Provincial Government recently decided to restore the porcelain production and sales tax (excerpt). Regarding the future of the porcelain industry, the industry was convened to discuss at a meeting. In this time of natural disasters and man-made disasters, when people are struggling to save themselves, how can they add heavy taxes to reduce their vitality? A unanimous resolution was passed to oppose the tax increase in Jiangxi Province. Porcelain is a major product of our country. In recent years, the people of the country have been frightened by the economic invasion of imperialists and have been seeking to promote it. There was originally an opportunity for development, but it was trapped by heavy taxes and tolls, which increased costs and made sales difficult. Foreigners were exempted from taxes and competed for sales, which led to foreign porcelain filling the country, especially Japanese goods. They have become the main force, and domestic porcelain has almost no foothold. Check the customs trade records, and the import of foreign porcelain has increased year by year, which is very alarming. The National Government saw the crux of the problem and proposed to reduce the tolls and increase the taxes. It resolutely issued an order to implement the toll reduction from the first day of the first month of the 20th year, sweeping away the malpractices that had plagued businesses and harmed the people for decades. The merchants and people cheered and hoped for the revival of the country. Unexpectedly, the Communist bandits were rampant and ravaged several provinces. Jingdezhen was repeatedly hit by bandit disasters, with cruel burning and killing. Last autumn, floods raged, and the people were in dire straits. Suffering was linked to suffering, reaching its extreme. The natural disaster had just been announced, and the national crisis struck again. Violent Japan took advantage of our natural disaster and sent troops to forcibly occupy the three northeastern provinces and attack Shanghai, which affected the whole country, and the economy was affected. Now, after the ceasefire and troop withdrawal, the people are deeply scarred and full of devastation. The government should try its best to appease the exiles and comfort the bereaved to seek recuperation, but Jiangxi suddenly has a proposal to restore the porcelain production and sales tax, which is like a disguised Lijin and seriously violates the National Government's order to reduce tolls. This cannot be recognized. In a country ruled by law, all increases and changes in taxes that increase the burden on the people must be based on laws and regulations. Jiangxi's tax increase this time has no laws and regulations from the central government, and it has a suspicion of violating the law and harming the people. This cannot be recognized. When foreigners are economically invading and conspiring to plot against us, people reduce and exempt taxes and compete for sales, while we increase taxes to block the development of domestic products, which is tantamount to suicide. This cannot be recognized. Now, after the natural disasters and bandit disasters, there are remnants and the national crisis. The people's livelihood is haggard. How can we bear to add heavy taxes to destroy their vitality? This cannot be recognized. Since the violent Japanese invaded Shanghai on January 28 and fought for several months, the national economy has been affected. Porcelain merchants in various places owe Jingdezhen kiln owners money and cannot repay it. If taxes are increased again, it will be difficult to maintain. Kiln owners will stop production in conjunction, and hundreds of thousands of workers will lose their jobs, endangering the livelihoods of the common people. This cannot be recognized. Moreover, porcelain merchants from various provinces handle goods with no fixed itinerary and are itinerant in nature. Therefore, there are no tax items for business tax, which shows that the national government can sympathize with the people's suffering, but the local government cannot uphold the virtues and intentions and instead destroy and plunder, which is extremely harmful to the people's livelihood. It is urgent to beg your association to give assistance and quickly forward it to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Finance and Industry of the National Government, ordering the Jiangxi Provincial Government to abide by the National Government's order and abolish the restoration of porcelain production and sales taxes similar to Lijin in order to value the law and protect the business community. Waiting for orders anxiously. Respectfully presented.

He reported on the purpose of the meeting and the progress of the association in the past year. Then, Qian Qinghao, a member of the Western District, reported on the Xieqiao fire and the case where the Second District did not report to the association. It was resolved that after sending a letter to the Second District, local interests would be the priority in the future, and the police would be reported as soon as possible. He Yongsheng, the director of the Eastern District, proposed to change the award certificate to a silver shield medal, which was approved. The chairman proposed whether the medal should be exchanged, which was resolved not to be exchanged. By the time the meeting was adjourned, the clock had struck four.

Store Silk and Wait for a Good Price 189

The sluggishness of the silk market in this port's foreign firms has reached its extreme. Chinese silk merchants are all in a situation where they will never recover. Recently, the spot silk in Lyon has shown some activity, and Shanghai white factory warp B pattern textiles have risen from more than 400 taels to more than 500 taels, but the silk market is still holding steady. Yesterday, according to a certain factory silk merchant, the reason for this is that the total amount of silk stored in Shanghai warehouses has reached 30,000 to 40,000 bales. Even in terms of white factory warp, the cost of the silk for the owners is more than 1,000 taels. After entrusting the silk number to sell the silk, the advance money of 800 to 900 taels has been used up (silk numbers and silk warehouses that sell factory warp and other silk in Shanghai usually advance money). Because the foreign firms were stagnant and difficult to sell for a while, the silk numbers mortgaged the silk to the financial industry, and each bale was also mortgaged for 600 to 700 taels of silver. Now, although the price of silk has risen to more than 500 taels, it is still not enough to cover the principal and interest of the mortgage, as well as warehouse rent, insurance, and other expenses. There is still a difference of more than 200 taels. If it is sold at the current market price, the owner will not only lose money but also have to pay off the advance money of the silk number and the insufficient principal and interest of the financial industry. Therefore, both the owner and the silk number are unwilling to sell immediately and insist on keeping the goods on hold, willing to add discount interest to wait for the opportunity. Seeing this, if the price increase of the foreign silk market is not high, there is no possibility of a smooth transition for a while.

Hongkou Chang'an Lane Tenants Petition Landlord for Rent Reduction Yesterday 190

Tenants of Chang'an Lane on Wusong Road, Hongkou, after establishing the Rent Reduction Movement Committee, submitted a request to the Municipal Rent Reduction Committee, asking them to negotiate with the landlord, the Catholic Church, for the exemption of rent during the war. Yesterday, all the tenants of the lane jointly petitioned the landlord, the Catholic Church, because Rongye Lane and Public Security Lane nearby have already had notices posted by their landlords, Jardine Matheson and Company and Kung Ho Yanghang, voluntarily exempting rent for three months, but this lane has not yet implemented this. We have always paid the rent on time without any disputes. Unexpectedly, the catastrophe of January 28th arrived this year, and the Hongkou area became a war zone. This lane was especially important. During the war, the tenants fled in a hurry, and thanks to the grace of the landlord, they were able to escape with their lives. However, although their lives were saved, their property was plundered by demons. All of this is evident to everyone. Recently, the ceasefire agreement has been reached, and we have had to move back to our original homes. The walls are bare, and the essence has been lost. The tenants are in pain and do not want to live after suffering this catastrophe. At this time, landlords in various lanes of the city, out of consideration for the tenants, have voluntarily exempted rent to show their generosity. Only this lane has not implemented it. The tenants have requested your church, but it has not been approved. Even the rent for January and May has not been collected by anyone. We do not know what the intention is. We hereby jointly petition again, and sincerely request your church to follow the compassionate will of our Lord, have a heart for helping the needy, and immediately exempt the rent for February, March, and April during the war in this lane. As for the rent for January and May before and after, we will do our best to pay it in order to express our gratitude. We cry and plead, and await your review." In addition, the tenants of the lane believe that the rent for February, March, and April should be exempted, but the landlord has not collected the rent for January and May before and after. They fear that the landlord will falsely accuse them of resisting rent and file a lawsuit in court. Therefore, they reported it to the Municipal Rent Reduction Committee to forward it to the Special District Court for filing to prevent deception. At the same time, they remitted the rent for January, May, and February to the bank for safekeeping, waiting for a solution.

Page 16

Lawyer Zhang Shizhao's Argument on the Yuansheng Case

Shareholders Yu Shouzheng and Luo Kunxiang of Yuansheng Gold Shop sued the general manager and shareholder Shi Zian, and shareholder Tian Hongnian, for jointly breaching trust and embezzlement. The First Special District Court has repeatedly summoned them. Qian Hongye, the presiding judge, announced the verdict in court the day before yesterday (the 22nd). Shi Zian and Tian Hongnian were found guilty of jointly breaching trust and were each fined 1,000 yuan. If they fail to pay the fine, they will be sentenced to imprisonment for one day for every three yuan. The part concerning Shou Fuchen was not accepted (in this part of the case, the plaintiff had withdrawn the case in court). The incidental civil lawsuit part was transferred to the civil division of this court for trial. The above information has been recorded in this newspaper. It is understood that the subject matter of this case involves a huge sum of more than 240,000 yuan. Both parties are well-known figures in the gold industry, and the lawsuit has attracted much attention from society. The first instance has been judged, and it cannot be said that it has not come to an end. Lawyer Zhang Shizhao is the agent for the plaintiff. Now we have obtained Lawyer Zhang's argument on the 15th and publish it as follows. It is believed that those who pay attention to social news will be happy to read it.

In terms of appearance, this case seems to belong to civil affairs, but tracing the details of its construction and the circumstances of the parties' confrontation, it is clearly a serious criminal case that goes beyond the ordinary. There is no doubt about this. Why do I say this? If Shi Zian, as the manager, accidentally made a mistake, resulting in some losses in the shop (regardless of the amount), he should have tried his best to prevent it beforehand, reported it to the shareholders in time, and then worked with the shareholders to plan for the aftermath, taking the lead in the difficult situation, and providing all the existing funds in the shop to jointly consider the priorities and repay the debts. If this were the case, he could have filed a lawsuit to pursue all the losses, regardless of who should be held responsible. This would truly be a civil lawsuit. If we speculate, at that time, Shi Zian would have gained the considerable sympathy of the shareholders, and based on the principle of forgiveness, a plan to settle the matter would have been devised. The case may have been settled through private mediation, and it would have been impossible to predict that it would be prosecuted. But now, according to the facts, it is very different. Shi Zian has been the general manager of Yuansheng Shop for many years. The following five points are worthy of consideration. Zian is experienced in handling affairs and worthy of the word "seasoned." He never accommodates customers, and even shareholders who come to the shop to buy and sell must follow the rules strictly. However, he is unique in treating Tian Hongnian differently, allowing him to lose more than 200,000 yuan without any prevention. This is the first point. Yuansheng has been thriving for four years and has had profits every year. Only the shortest period after August last year was reported as a loss. How much was lost is all on the books, which is the more than 200,000 yuan that Zian admitted was owed by Tian Hongnian. Where did the 50,000 taels of capital and several tens of thousands of yuan of accumulated profits go? This is the second point. Yuansheng suffered because of Tian Hongnian alone. Hongnian is his brother-in-law and also the manager of the China Exchange Bank. Zian indulged in kinship and was intimidated by his power, colluding with him to seek unexpected wealth and diverting funds from the China Exchange Bank to cover his losses. This is the third point. Everyone in the shop, from the general manager down, is Shi and Tian's confidants. Yu Shouzheng and other shareholders have never been involved in the shop's affairs from the beginning. This is the fourth point. Those who do business on the exchange often establish accounts, which easily lead to fraud and confusion. This is obvious to everyone. Now, Tian Hongnian has established as many as seven or eight accounts, such as Hongji, Huifu, Jinji, Pinji, Hongji, Deji, and Nongji. Shi Zian allowed him to do so without preventing him. The traces of collusion are obvious. This is the fifth point. Based on these five points, Shi and Tian lost more than 200,000 yuan. What kind of blame should they bear? Even a fool can understand this. When the shop was in urgent need of funds and the China Exchange Bank was pressing for the repayment of debts, Zian suddenly fled, claiming that "the China Exchange Bank's matter was about to take direct action against me. I am unable to cope with my sick body and have no choice but to temporarily retreat in order to protect myself and gain time." (See lawyer Yuan Yang'an's letter of January 18.) If the China Exchange Bank were to take direct action against Zian, Zian's escape would inevitably lead to direct action against other shareholders due to joint liability. How could Zian not know this? As a result, Yu Shouzheng and others returned 150,000 yuan to the China Exchange Bank, and the matter was resolved. This is in line with the meaning of Article 366 of the Criminal Law, "Intending to cause illegal damage to oneself, and acting in violation of one's duties, resulting in damage to one's property." There is absolutely no doubt. The letter also says, "I have no choice but to temporarily retreat in order to protect myself." The original text of the Criminal Law regarding "handling affairs for others" caused huge losses, and the cause of the huge losses was entirely due to himself. In the end, he escaped and claimed to be protecting himself. Everyone wants to protect themselves. Now, the person who caused the disaster is using self-protection as an excuse to leave, causing the third party who was entrusted to him and does not ask questions to be unable to protect himself, resulting in a huge sacrifice. This is so obvious that he intends to harm others for his own benefit. This constitutes a crime of violating his duties, which is so serious. The aforementioned Yuansheng's capital and accumulated profits were all spent by Zian alone. According to Article 356 of the Criminal Law, "Intending to illegally possess for oneself or a third party property owned by others that one holds." How fitting is this? In short, Shi Zian advertised himself as being serious about his work, so that the shareholders mistakenly regarded him as someone they could always rely on, and entrusted the shop's affairs to him completely without ever questioning him. This is the extreme of "trusting" Zian. Zian then "betrayed" them, and the extent of his betrayal was inversely proportional to the shareholders' trust in him. His crime is a thorough and vivid explanation of the word "breach of trust" in the Criminal Law. The law emphasizes the intention to punish. Zian's intention can be said to be extremely vicious. All of these facts are enough to embellish this case and make it a major criminal case, and that's not all. After the shop closed down, Shi Zian still concealed the only remaining funds in the shop, dared to establish a private account, deposit it in Hongxiang Qianzhuang, and then privately withdrew a part of it for free distribution according to his own will, and secretly sent letters to his partners Song Fuchen and others, ordering them to quickly divide the money to prevent the shareholders from knowing and confiscating the money. When the China Exchange Bank's huge debts were about to affect the shareholders, Zian saw it very clearly. He had to destroy every last bit of the remaining amount to make himself happy. In other words, Zian was afraid that the shareholders would not bear the obligations that they should not bear, and he was afraid that the shareholders would not enjoy the rights that they should enjoy. Such a state of mind is something that even ordinary petty people cannot bear to do. According to the law, how high did Zian's intention to embezzle reach? I believe that the presiding judge will be shocked by his free conscience. Who would say that it is not appropriate to call it a serious criminal case? The money in Hongxiang is also an occasional discovery of Zian's total embezzlement. It is not difficult to estimate that there are still many undiscovered ones. When he secretly deposited the remaining money in Hongxiang, he refused to reveal any traces to the shareholders. If the shareholders had no way to detect the crime and did not know about this money, Zian would have immediately taken it for himself and embezzled it to the end. It goes without saying. When the matter was exposed, Zian lied and said that it was other people's deposit and the dividends that the partners should have received. What is the harm in letting the shareholders know about other people's deposits and the dividends that the partners should have received, which are part of the shop's debts? Saying that the shareholders will only collect "debts owed to them" and not care about "debts they owe" is evidenced by the character and behavior of the shareholders that Zian knew and the facts before and after. Even if he lost all conscience, I am afraid he could not say this. Moreover, the so-called partner dividends have already been offset by outstanding debts. In fact, the money is no longer there. Since the money is only a nominal amount, Zian took the actual money away. Finally, under the repeated requests of his partners, Yu Shouzheng still advanced more than 2,300 yuan to them (receipt submitted to the court). It can be seen that the shareholders will never let people down. Now Zian's remarks are nothing more than an attempt to cover up his crimes and add more lies, which is exactly this kind of thing. Moreover, Tian Hongnian engaged in public bonds in Yuansheng. If he won, he would take the money out. If he lost, he would leave it there. Although it is now said to be a loss, how much has accumulated and gone away still needs to be investigated. Also, in the names of various accounts, such as Pinji, etc., he made for others, taking a share of the profits as the price of bearing responsibility. There is no way to know clearly. Shi Zian is extremely clever and accustomed to stealing while guarding. If he said that he was involved in the lawsuit by others, I would become a rich man on my own. Judging from his behavior, he seems to have the determination to endure torture and deny it. This phrase "intending to obtain illegal benefits for oneself or a third party" in the law is truly thorough. Who is the third party? From Shi Zian's point of view, it is Tian Hongnian. From Tian Hongnian's point of view, it is Shi Zian. The traces of the two helping each other to make profits and colluding with each other have been consistent from the beginning and have not changed. Although their accounts are intertwined, Tian does not admit that the losses are so huge. This is the constant state of these people devouring each other for profit, which is not surprising. In short, when Shi and Tian brewed their crimes, one was the general manager of Yuansheng and the other was the manager of the China Exchange Bank. Both had the power to do evil easily. As the facts show, they committed crimes and offenses, using the power they possessed to the fullest extent. If such cunning and illegal people commit crimes such as embezzlement, breach of trust, and fraud, and if the harm suffered by their peers is so clear, and if the law does not provide adequate relief, and if the offenders are not punished with the applicable criminal articles, it will be seen that honest and honest merchants in Shanghai will no longer have a foothold in the future. The belief that society looks up to the court as a refuge will also be shaken. People like Yu Shouzheng run their businesses with a purely old-fashioned style, with credit as their second life. In order to preserve credit, they will not hesitate to go bankrupt. In the common business practices, 150,000 yuan should be returned to the China Exchange Bank, and it can be done by opening the books. However, Yu and others did not want to do this. Shi and Tian dared to use the China Exchange Bank to threaten Yu and others, forcing them to repay the expenses of failed speculation with their own hard-earned money. They were simply taking advantage of Yu and others' integrity, morality, and various good qualities to achieve unspeakable motives. Recently, customs have become lax, and human morality has deteriorated. The situation is even worse in the Shanghai foreign concession. Those who have a heart are truly worried. The aforementioned good qualities are extremely easy to destroy, but extremely difficult to cultivate. It is fortunate that there are still merchants like Yu who follow their duties and are diligent. It cannot be said that it is not difficult and commendable. If the law cannot protect them, so that the place where good people do good deeds becomes a stepping stone for evil people to commit crimes, and the crimes committed by them make the good-doers feel discouraged and unwilling to do more, or even if they intend to do so, they are too exhausted to start. Specifically, the word joint liability for future partnerships will become an empty word in the legal dictionary, with no facts to corroborate it. What will be the impact of this on people's hearts, customs, industry, and all other industries? This lawyer is secretly afraid of this, so he dares to state his humble opinions in detail, providing them to the presiding judge for reference. Recently, there is a bad trend in Shanghai, where civil cases are used to falsely accuse criminal lawsuits as a means of intimidation and extortion. This lawyer secretly disapproves of this. However, if it is clearly a criminal case, and it is deliberately placed in the ranks of civil cases in order to gain fame and reputation, this kind of overcorrection is also something that this lawyer does not agree with. Excessive is as bad as inadequate and does not serve the purpose. It is necessary to follow the name and demand the reality, and only be correct. The fact that this case belongs to criminal affairs and is a case with conclusive evidence is undoubtedly beyond doubt. I propose that your court punish Shi Zian and Tian Hongnian according to the seriousness of the case as a warning to the cunning and illegal. Song Fuchen colluded in fraud and the circumstances were lighter. What crime should he be charged with? Your court will certainly have the power to weigh it. This lawyer does not dare to presume to ask. As for the incidental civil lawsuit, I also ask that Shi and others be held fully responsible, that Yu Shouzheng and others'代偿debts and the remaining outstanding debts of Yuansheng Shop be paid in full with interest, and that all litigation costs be borne by the defendants. This is truly beneficial for both public and private morality.

Woman Accuses Husband of Bigamy 193

Defendant Failed to Appear in Court Yesterday

Court Orders Plaintiff to Summon

Ding Hexue, a woman from Fengxian County, Pudong, is now 31 years old. She recently retained lawyer Zhu Honglie to file a criminal complaint with the First Special District Court against her husband, Xu Zushen, for bigamy with a woman named Fei Xuehua. The complaint stated that Ding and Xu were formally married in October of the 11th year of the Republic of China according to the lunar calendar, and it has been ten years. Their feelings have never been compatible, because Xu went to study in Peiping after the marriage and never returned home, so that there have been no children to this day. In the 17th year of the Republic of China, after Xu came south from Peiping, he lived in Shanghai, occasionally returning home, but always received a cold shoulder and harsh words. Therefore, they only bear the empty name of husband and wife. Xu actually intensified his efforts, and on the 28th day of the third month of the lunar calendar last year, he brought Fei and her two daughters home, as if they were husband and wife, and regarded the plaintiff as a stranger. Such a break in love is too difficult to bear. After repeated investigations, it was discovered that the defendants had formally married in Jinglin Hall on Kunshan Road in Shanghai in April of the 18th year of the Republic of China, and even dared to hold a large banquet to invite relatives and friends to celebrate. The only person who was deceived was the plaintiff. Therefore, she came to the court to file a lawsuit, requesting a summons to be issued to punish them according to law, and incidentally filed a civil lawsuit, ordering Xu to pay alimony of 10,800 yuan at one time (30 yuan per month, calculated for 30 years), as well as 5,000 yuan for dowry and compensation for losses. The court approved the complaint and ordered a summons to be issued. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Qiao Wanxuan came to court to gather information. The defendants Xu Zushen and Fei Xuehua did not arrive. The Chinese police reported that they went to Cuichang Pawnshop on North Henan Road to serve the summons to the two defendants, but there was no Cuichang Pawnshop there, so they were unable to deliver the summons. The plaintiff's agent, lawyer Zhu, then stated that according to Article 339 of the Criminal Procedure Law, spouses may not file a complaint themselves, so he requested that the police station be instructed to file a joint complaint. Judge Qiao said that according to the agreement, the court did not have this authority. Then he briefly questioned the plaintiff Ding Hexue. Ding was fat, her appearance was not bad, she had short hair and was dressed in modern fashion. She said that the two defendants used to live in Pudong and now live in Cuichang Pawnshop on Baker Road. Judge Qiao verified the confession and instructed that the case be postponed for seven days, waiting for the plaintiff to summon the defendants to court for verification.

Rent Reduction Movement Update Yesterday 198

Gonghe Road Zhen'an Lane on Gonghe Road in Zhabei has more than 300 buildings, close to the railway and in a dangerous war zone. Because the landlord, Kunji Company, did not show any consideration, they took the opportunity to issue a notice when the tenants were returning one after another, collecting rent "from May." Not only could the rent during the war (February, March, April, and May, four months) not be completely waived, but all old debts had to be paid as usual, and there was no reduction in the new rent. Otherwise, they would have to transfer the lease. The tenants could not afford to bear it after surviving the disaster. Therefore, they were represented by Liu Wenbin, Liu Hongdao, and Wu Gongtui to appeal to the Social Affairs Bureau's Municipal Rent Reduction Movement Committee and the Shanghai Tenants' General Federation, asking for help. Lawyers Huang Xiubo and others, entrusted by the Rent Reduction Committee and this association, sent warning letters, but the company ignored them and continued to force the collection of rent with the police. The representative Liu Hongdao and others immediately sought the consent of all the tenants in the lane and established a preparatory committee for the Tenants' Union at No. 120 in this lane yesterday. Liu Wenbin, Zhang Minxian, Liu Hongdao, Zhao Fulin, Wu Gongtui, Han Guifu, Cheng Guoan, Cheng Dasan, Wu Yingxing, Gu Jieran, He Yucai, Dai Minghua, and Xu Shentai and other thirteen people were appointed as executive committee members. The personnel for the supervisory, alternate, and secretary positions were also largely determined. The following resolutions were made regarding the progress of the rent reduction issue: (1) Measures (1) Postpone the payment of old debts, (2) Waive all rent during the war (February, March, April, and May, four months), (3) Pay 50% from June to the end of the year, (2) Request the Rent Reduction Movement Committee to mediate, (3) Hold an inaugural meeting on a regular basis and invite members from the Rent Reduction Committee, the Tenant's General Federation, and the Commercial Federation to provide guidance, (4) Before the Municipal Government's Rent Reduction Measures are announced, all rents will be paid slowly. The method of depositing the rent in the bank will be discussed at the inaugural meeting.

Chengren Lane Chengren Lane at the corner of Zhongxing Road and Datong Road in Zhabei has dozens of city houses, which are the property of Chengren Company. The rental accountant is urging tenants to pay the rent owed before the war, and also demanding that each room pay an additional two yuan for water because the tenants use too much water. The tenants convened a meeting of all tenants at around 9 AM yesterday to discuss the matter. First, the tenants reported the above-mentioned losses and their difficult circumstances, and requested the landlord to waive the rent for February, March, April, and May (four months), and to reduce the monthly rent by 30% from June to the end of the year. However, the landlord's representative, Shangguan Rong, believed that it was reasonable to waive the rent for February, March, April, and May (four months), but could not agree to the 30% rent reduction and had to ask the landlord for instructions. Next, they discussed adding two yuan per month for water to each room. In the end, the mediation determined that the tenants' water consumption should be calculated at 10% of the rent. For example, a 10-yuan rent can only use one yuan of water per month, and a 20-yuan rent can use two yuan of water. The rest can be deduced by analogy. If this limit is exceeded, the excess water fee should be shared by the tenants. As a result, all the tenants did not agree because the packaged water system did not have this method. The meeting ended without a result.

Record of the Meeting of the Beijing Road Businessmen's Association 199

The Beijing Road Businessmen's Association held a committee meeting yesterday, presided over by Chairman Zhang Yichen, to discuss (1) the case of member Hengtai's new Han Bang store, whose landlord, under the pretext of rent arrears, coerced them to move; a resolution was passed: A. In addition to the rent for February and March, the remaining rent should be deposited in the bank; B. Letters should be sent to various sectors for assistance; (2) how to handle the case of the Concession telephone company taking the opportunity to increase prices; a resolution was passed: reject the price increase and notify all members to join the Telephone Users' Association; (3) how to proceed with the National Crisis Savings Fund; a resolution was passed: submit to the General Membership Meeting; (4) the reduction and exemption of rent in this city has been pending for a long time, while Jing, Hang, and other places have already received government orders to implement rent reduction; the unique case of this city that remains unresolved causes more disputes; how to handle this case; a resolution was passed: send a letter to the Rent Reduction and Exemption Association, convene another city-wide representative conference for public resolution, and then submit it to the municipal government for a prompt decision on rent reduction and exemption measures; (5) the case of re-registering members of this association; a resolution was passed: promote Tong Huitang, Yang Guangxing, and Zhou Hongquan to be responsible for handling.

Letter Received 208

Dear Editor, Respectfully, I have just read your newspaper's report on the "Japanese Manufacturing Morphine Case" and I am extremely shocked. According to this pharmacy, it was established in the 15th year of the Republic by doctors and well-known figures in the business community who invested together. It is entirely a company with the nature that its business objectives are in accordance with the regulations of the Ministry of Health for the management of Western medicine enterprises, and there are absolutely no transgressions. As for Ye Junqinghe, he is only one of the shareholders of this company, and his individual actions have nothing to do with this company. Moreover, although Ye Jun was falsely accused of being a suspect, he was also questioned by the First and Second Courts of the Shanghai Special District. As a result, the false accusation was found to be unsubstantiated, and he was released on bail pending further evidence. Looking at the above points, it can be seen that this case has nothing to do with this company. We are afraid that people from all walks of life will not understand the truth and that misunderstandings will lead to a significant impact on the company's reputation, so we have specially sent this letter to you, hoping that you will correct it as soon as possible. We would be most grateful. Yours sincerely,

To the Editor, In yesterday's local news in your newspaper, it was reported that a young man named Lu Zhongyi committed suicide by poison in the Shanghai Hotel, leaving behind a photo with the words "Nantong Jiangsu Bank Communications Office" written on the back. Today's follow-up news stated that the deceased was Li Zhongyi, etc. After investigation, there is no such person in our Nantong branch. It is unknown whether the deceased has any relatives or friends among the employees of our bank. In addition to sending a letter to our bank for investigation, we also request that you publish this letter in the "Letters to the Editor" column to avoid inaccurate rumors. Yours sincerely, General Administration Office of Jiangsu Bank, June 23.
