Supplement to the Shanghai Shenbao

Arts and Literature

Preface to the Credit Recording of the Songjiang National Crisis Temporary Relief Association 209

— Lu Gui Liang

The planes are rumbling, the cannons are booming, people are panicking, and the refugees are thronging. This was the actual state of Songjiang society in early February. I, together with gentlemen from my hometown, gathered to discuss, raised donations separately, contacted Shen, accommodated and set up places. Thanks to everyone's efforts, we succeeded. The refugees received numbered from dozens to hundreds to over two thousand. The donations raised went from dozens to hundreds to over six thousand. As there were many refugees, the house was small and difficult to accommodate, so there were one place, two places, and three places. Their earnest willingness to contribute their talents, money, rice, meat and vegetarian food, clothing, and other miscellaneous items to the association was evident. In terms of groups, there were the business community, academia, the political world, the military world, and the police world. In terms of the general public, there were the old, the young, men, women, converts to Buddhism, and believers in Catholicism and Christianity. Everyone contributed their mental strength, financial resources, eloquence, and talents. They responded to each other and moved in the same direction, unanimously agreeing and helping each other. The hearts of the people of Songjiang can be said to be united. Is there any other effect? It is because the violent Japanese are invading, and disaster will come at any time. Fellow countrymen are suffering, and their pain is related to us. It is all rooted in the conscience of loving others and originates from the innate goodness of human nature, and it cannot be helped. However, I deeply feel that this time, the Japanese invaders did not reach Songjiang, but those received in the institute were mostly from eastern Zhejiang, northern Jiangsu (workers in yarn factories), Baoshan and Jiading in Suzhou, and the Zhabei and Jiangwan areas of Shanghai (business and agricultural circles). The relief association operated and arranged for only one hundred and one days, and only more than four thousand eight hundred yuan were used. There was enough manpower, and the warehouse had enough money. It can be said to be fortunate in misfortune. Today, there is no guiding principle at the top and no law to follow at the bottom. Internal worries arise one after another, and foreign troubles occur frequently. Looking around in horror, I am quietly worried. If all my colleagues in the community can be honest with themselves and love others, endure hardship and fulfill their responsibilities, use their enthusiasm to help those in need, spend their surplus wealth to help the poor, broaden their horizons, and help each other regardless of regional boundaries, then even if there are disturbances from party bandits, rampant petty people, and all kinds of incredible changes, we will have the strength to deal with them, and the disaster can be slightly reduced. What do you think of this, gentlemen of virtue?

Science

New Wireless Radio (Continued) 210

— Nai Zheng

Speaking of the inside of it, because the new radio puts various components together, it is very complicated, but most of them are tightly placed, saving a lot of space. However, the positions of each component have been precisely designed by radio engineers, and they are not arbitrarily piled up inside. As for the structure of the coil, the sufficient gap between each component, and the correct distance, they were all carefully considered in the design beforehand. Therefore, the difficulties caused by magneto-electric cooperation and electrostatic cooperation have also been reduced, and various noisy sounds have also been changed. As for the speaker (or amplifier), the latest radio uses a new type of dynamic amplifier, which emits clear and loud tones, which cannot be compared with old-fashioned speakers. It is also placed inside.

The convenience of the new radio lies in the use of alternating current. The reason why it can use alternating current has to be attributed to a new invention of vacuum tubes. It uses low-voltage alternating current to supply the burning of the filament. However, there is also a type of battery vacuum tube. Although low-voltage alternating current can make the filament glow red, it does not generate any effect. It must be directly connected to a device that converts alternating current into direct current (this device is called a B-type rectifier) before supplying the filament. Almost all new radios on the market now use alternating current vacuum tubes.

Science is an ever-changing and progressing field, and wireless electricity is advancing even more rapidly. In other countries, new radios have long been available in every household, enjoying the knowledge and entertainment provided by wireless electricity. In the United States, it is even more developed. There are now seven or eight companies broadcasting wireless movies (Television). This type of radio that can only listen and not watch has long become a thing of the past. Therefore, foreign manufacturers transport them to our country, which only knows how to enjoy and does not know how to manufacture them, for special sales. Although its price has dropped a lot since this year, we are still handing over hundreds of yuan to foreigners with both hands when we buy a radio. The outflow of money is truly heartbreaking. I hope that manufacturers in our country will quickly imitate it and recover our rights and interests (end).

Sexual Issues

Incredible Things 211

— Yi Yong

Miss ×× committed suicide by jumping into the river because her spinsterhood ideals were not achieved! This news spread throughout our M village.

The fact is this: Miss ×× was betrothed by her parents to a farming family in the same village since she was a child. Recently, Miss ××'s husband's family proposed to get married, and the auspicious day had been chosen. Unexpectedly, Miss ×× committed suicide a week before she was about to get married, leaving a suicide note stating that she vowed not to marry anyone, and that she had no choice but to take this measure because her parents did not allow it. When her parents were busily preparing her dowry, they discovered this news and fainted again and again with grief.

A few days later, my little sister and I went to Shen for something. Suddenly, we saw Miss ×× wearing a fashionable outfit, and also with a Western-dressed young man, arm in arm, talking and laughing as they stepped into the ×× movie theater. I was confused at the time. Driven by curiosity, I secretly followed them closely.

"I pretended to jump into the river for you, I voluntarily alienated my parents for you, I risked the bad name of being unfilial for you, I for you..." Miss ×× said, leaning her head a little on the young man's shoulder.

"Oh my Dearest, I know everything. You sacrificed everything for me, and of course I am willing to sacrifice everything for you. Let's leave Shanghai quickly tomorrow. After a month, we can live together to consummate our love," the Western-dressed young man said softly, stroking Miss ××'s fingers.

After listening to their conversation, I finally woke up from a dream and suddenly realized. But my little sister pulled my hand and insisted that I leave quickly, so I silently walked to the place we wanted to go.

A Small and Strange Thing

Tangbing Feast 212

— Tian Fang

My friend Lao Wang had a son, and yesterday he sent me an invitation and a box of red eggs, eight of them. The invitation read:

"I respectfully choose ×month ×day as the day for the full moon of my young son ××. I will respectfully prepare Tangbing (noodles served at a baby's first month party). I respectfully invite your whole family to come!" Underneath was "×× bows" and "The banquet will be held at ×× Restaurant."

I don't understand, why does he want to invite people to drink when his child is born? If it's for celebration, then what is being celebrated? If it's for "adding a male heir," it's still a question of whether adding a male heir is a good thing. Moreover, most of the common people who are happy to have children are made into cannon fodder or fill the ditches. In the past twenty years, due to natural disasters and man-made disasters, the population has lost an unknown amount. The soldiers sacrificed in the Battle of Longhai are enough to build a small country. If it is said to be "both wealth and offspring flourishing" and "celebration for the family," then how do you know that this child will definitely seek welfare for the country and become a great man for society in the future? Maybe he will degenerate or betray the country and become a traitorous businessman and be scolded by future generations? Therefore, even if you want to celebrate, it should be on the day of "success and fame," and definitely not on the day of the full moon. Furthermore, if you want to take this opportunity to have a drink with a few friends, then a "potluck" is fine, why use the child as a topic? I send gifts, and you host a banquet, which is not economical for both of us, and only benefits the silver shop and the liquor store? It is better to use the banquet fee for the Tangbing party to cultivate yourself and other children, then wouldn't the future celebration be more reliable? In short, I can't find the ultimate thing worth celebrating in this matter, or the reason why I should be invited to drink. If there is, there is one more decorative item, a toy, in the family. Like adding a gramophone or a talking parrot, it is a pastime for the father and grandparents. Another meaning is to take this opportunity to "show off" in front of friends. In short, it has nothing to do with the ignorant child. This is a game for wealthy adults.

Treating children as decorative items like potted plants in the family, or toys like pet cats and dogs, is terrible for the children. If I were a child, I would protest.

Page 18

Startling

Lessons from Watching a Slapstick Play 213

— He Zhou

The ×× slapstick troupe was performing at the ×× theater. A friend came to pull me to see it. To relieve the boredom of my spare time, I finally stepped into the entertainment arena, which I hadn't set foot in for five months.

The name of the play was "The First Bridge in the World," which was a cameo performance of juggling. It was the so-called "360 lines of business." Of course, what the actors on stage were performing made people unable to help but laugh. In particular, the wit of the dialogue gave me a profound hint. Although what they said was all in "slapstick" tone, it was not just for people to "laugh." It also contained a teaching meaning.

The stage was set like this: A beggar was singing loudly. A passerby saw him and said with a cold taunt and disgusted tone, "Poor beggar! You're so poor, and you still want to be so happy!"

The beggar heard this and retorted, "Don't look down on the poor in a condescending way. Maybe you will end up like me in the future."

The passerby glared at the beggar for a while and then said proudly, "Bah! I have fine clothes and good food, money and power. How can I be poor?"

"Hum! Your current position is exactly my past life." The beggar said in a frivolous tone, calmly and with emotion, "Hehe! Let me tell you, I used to be even more prominent than you! But it's the second time I've become a beggar."

The beggar then said in a regretful tone, "I was originally a poor beggar. Later, I was pitied and taken in by someone, and I slowly improved. Before long, I was able to stand on my own. So I married a wife and bought a house, and everything went smoothly. I earned some money and started speculating in business. As a result, I luckily won. At this time, it was no longer the same. I built a Western-style house, bought a car, and took in beautiful concubines, doing everything one by one. I looked down on all my old poor friends. It's just like you looking down on me now. I saw those dignitaries and nobles and flattered them a lot, because I felt that with them, I would have a backer and could do anything recklessly. At that time, I had a considerable reputation. Occasionally, I did a sloppy event, and no one could do anything to me. I was really carefree, eating, drinking, and hanging out all day long. There was no day that I didn't go to dance halls and gambling dens. I spent all day living the life of a 'big boss.' Who knew that the affairs of the world could not escape the fixed rule of circulation. I was in 'wealth' and only circled half a circle. After all, money is limited, and fate is limited. Later, because I did a bribery affair, I was accused. So I ate lawsuits. Eating lawsuits depends on whether you have a wide range of connections. The other party was better than me, and I was already in the wrong. In the end, I was imprisoned, my family property was confiscated, my reputation was ruined, and I had nowhere to go. Thinking about it, it was as if I had taken a bath in society. In the end, I still ended up like this, returning to my original appearance and still living as a beggar... So you are now complacent and arrogant, which is really unconscious." After the beggar finished speaking, he gave a sinister laugh.

"..." The passerby thought for a while and then said with enlightenment, "The rich should not look down on the poor, and the poor should not be jealous of the rich."

A word led me, sitting under the stage, to sigh secretly.

Shanghai First Special District Local Court 216

Civil First Instance Judgments:

Xu Wenbin vs. Zhou Weibin Rent Arrears Case: 217

The defendant shall compensate the plaintiff 360 taels of silver and 21 yuan in silver dollars and vacate the premises. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

Hui Zhong Bank General Manager Mark vs. Markdekov et al. Debt Case: 218

The defendant Markdekov shall repay the plaintiff 179 yuan and interest at the rate of 1% per month from the date of the lawsuit until the date of repayment. If he is unable to repay, the defendant Fultoff shall repay on his behalf. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

Xia Keshen vs. Jin Renquan et al. Debt Case: 219

The defendant Jin Renquan shall repay the plaintiff 100 yuan. This amount shall be repaid at a rate of 10 yuan per month until fully paid. If he is unable to repay, the defendant Zhenli Company shall repay on his behalf. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

Solde Sheng vs. Bai Yunqing et al. Debt Case: 220

The defendants shall jointly and severally repay the plaintiff 40 yuan. This amount shall be jointly and severally repaid at a rate of 7 yuan per month until fully paid. The litigation costs shall be jointly and severally borne by the defendants.

Mao Lianghong vs. Tang Yin et al. Rent Arrears Case: 221

The defendant Tang Yin shall return the rented furniture and pay the rent from January to May to the plaintiff. If he is unable to repay, Chen Juxing shall repay on his behalf. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

Miao Jinyong vs. Huang Shunkun et al. Debt Case: 222

The defendant Huang Shunkun shall repay the plaintiff 100 yuan. If he is unable to repay, the defendant Huang Yutang shall repay on his behalf. The litigation costs shall be borne by Huang Shunkun. The plaintiff's request for provisional execution is rejected.

Cao Yuncai vs. Dong Zhaosen Compensation Case: 223

The defendant shall return 170 yuan to the plaintiff. The plaintiff's other claims are rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne equally by both parties.

Qiang Sheng vs. Tian Renfu Loan Case: 224

The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 200 yuan. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

Feng He Zhuang et al. vs. Yong Ji owner Ke Meisun Rent Arrears Case: 225

The plaintiff's claim is rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff.

Fang Mingjie vs. Li Deqing Payment for Construction Costs Case: 226

The plaintiff's claim is rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff.

Ge Benchen, i.e., Ge Chenshi, vs. Ge Chengrong Divorce Case: 227

The marriage between the plaintiff and the defendant is granted a divorce. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

Xu Qiuzhi Tang Zhu Yanyuan vs. Xu Xitang Rent Arrears Case: 228

The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 154 yuan in rent. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. The plaintiff's other claims are rejected.

Kai Mu Xin vs. Ji Jianqing et al. Loan Case: 229

The defendant Ji Jianqing shall repay the plaintiff 100 yuan. This amount shall be repaid at a rate of 10 yuan per month until fully paid. If he is unable to repay, the defendant Peng Weigan shall repay on his behalf.

Wu Baoshi vs. Wu Runsheng Identity Confirmation Case: 230

It is confirmed that the defendant is not the adopted son of the plaintiff's deceased husband, Wu Meisheng. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

Dingyuan Cheng Silk Shop vs. Yuan Xixiang Foreign Goods Store Debt Case: 231

The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 124 yuan and 3 jiao and 4 fen, and 268 taels, 4 qian, and 4 fen of silver. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

Li Chaorui et al. vs. Longchang Tai Lie Ji Furniture Store Xu Zhilin Goods Payment Case: 232

The defendant shall jointly and severally repay the plaintiff Li Chaorui 402 yuan. The defendant shall jointly and severally repay the plaintiff Wang Maoxing 389 yuan and 7 jiao. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

Bao Zuoming vs. Su Longsun et al. Debt Case: 233

The defendant Su Longsun shall repay the plaintiff 99 yuan, 6 jiao, 1 fen, and 4 li. If he is unable to repay, the defendant Su Xingsun shall be liable for repayment. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant Su Longsun.

Chen Ruilin vs. Xiong Futang Transfer Price Case: 234

The defendant Xiong Futang shall immediately pay the plaintiff the transfer price of 370 yuan. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

Zhu Zilen vs. Miao Pengnian Debt Case: 235

The plaintiff's claim is rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff.

Amu Sheng vs. Sun Ahai et al. Loan Case: 236

The defendant Sun Ahai owes the plaintiff 320 yuan until fully paid. If he is unable to repay 100 yuan of the aforementioned debt, the defendant Tang Shengkui shall repay it on his behalf. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

Song Wenkui vs. Mao Huangshi et al. Subscription Fee Case: 237

The defendant Mao Huangshi shall repay the plaintiff 170 yuan. This amount shall be repaid in nine months, with 20 yuan per month and 10 yuan in the last month until fully paid. If she is unable to repay, the defendant Huang Baorong shall repay on her behalf. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

Tang Tianmin vs. Zhuo Jiliang et al. Loan Case: 238

The defendant Zhuo Jiliang shall repay the plaintiff 322 yuan, 5 jiao, and 6 fen, and interest at the rate of 1% per month from the date of the loan until the date of execution. If he is unable to repay, the defendant Guangtai Factory’s owners Zhang Hongfa and Zhenyuanxiang’s owner Zhu Shibiao shall repay on his behalf. The defendant Zhuo Jiliang shall repay the plaintiff 100 yuan and interest at the rate of 1% per month from the date of the loan until the date of execution. If he is unable to repay, the defendant Guangtai Factory’s owner Zhang Hongfa shall repay on his behalf. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

Zhang Zhenyang vs. Fan Bofan Debt Case: 239

The defendant shall repay the plaintiff’s principal of 20 yuan and interest of 11 yuan, 4 jiao, and 9 fen, and 9 li on behalf of Yao Sanbao. The plaintiff's other claims are rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

Zhao Xiu Ji vs. Jin Shungen et al. Loan Case: 240

The defendant Jin Shungen shall repay the plaintiff 1,000 yuan and interest at the rate of 1.5% per month from September 1, 1929, until the date of execution. If he is unable to repay, the defendant Zhu Caidi shall repay on his behalf. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

Xia Chenshi, i.e., A Mao, vs. Xia Guitang et al. Separation from Family Relationship and Return of Property Price Case: 241

The defendant shall allow the plaintiff to separate from the family relationship. The plaintiff's other claims are rejected. The litigation costs for the separation part shall be borne by the defendant, and the rest shall be borne by the plaintiff.

(Main text) Wei Jiade is sentenced to one month of imprisonment and a fine of 40 yuan for smoking opium. Pan Dongsheng is sentenced to one month of imprisonment and a fine of 40 yuan for assisting in smoking opium. If the fines are converted to imprisonment, one day is calculated for every two yuan. Zhang Zhifeng's petition for withdrawal is acknowledged. Since this case falls under the jurisdiction of the primary court and you do not wish the defendant to be punished, the case should be dismissed. This ruling. 326

Fei Liren's petition for withdrawal is acknowledged. After reviewing the case of Wang Xiao Guozhi's abduction filed by this person, it has not been proven that there was any violence. Since an out-of-court settlement has been reached, a dismissal should be granted immediately. This ruling. 328

Gu Jide's statement is acknowledged. You are hereby ordered to await investigation by the Public Security Bureau and not to make further requests. This ruling. 329

Sun Bao Yin's petition for record is acknowledged. There are no provisions for record in criminal cases. The request should not be considered. This ruling. 330

Dong Ta Hong's request for dismissal is acknowledged. After reviewing the case of your sister Zhou Dongshi's suicide, it has been confirmed that it was indeed a suicide and that Zhou Derong was not involved. The bruises around the right eye and the abrasion on the left rib are all crimes that require a complaint to be pursued. Since the relatives of Zhou have submitted a petition stating that they do not wish to pursue the matter, a dismissal should be granted. This ruling. 331
